id=\"caption-attachment-2131187\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"><strong>Image Credits:</strong> Nigel Sussman</p></div></p>\n<p>On Tuesday, we published a four-part series on Tonal, a home fitness startup that has raised $200 million since it launched in 2018. The company&#8217;s patented hardware combines digital weights, coaching and AI in a wall-mounted system that sells for $2,995.</p>\n<p>By any measure, it is poised for success — <strong>sales increased 800%</strong> between December 2019 and 2020, and by the end of this year, the company will have 60 retail locations. On Wednesday, <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/31/strength-training-startup-tonal-crosses-unicorn-status-after-raising-250m/\">Tonal reported a $250 million Series E</a> that valued the company at $1.6 billion.</p>\n<p>Our deep dive examines Tonal&#8217;s origins, product development timeline, its go-to-market strategy and other aspects that combined to spark investor interest and customer delight.</p>\n<p>We call this format the &#8220;<a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/ec-1/\">EC-1</a>,&#8221; since these stories are as comprehensive and illuminating as the S-1 forms startups must file with the SEC before going public.</p>\n<p>Here&#8217;s how the Tonal EC-1 breaks down:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>Part 1: <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/30/tonal-ec1-origin/\">How a homegrown experiment became one of the fastest-growing companies in fitness tech</a></li>\n<li>Part 2: <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/30/tonal-ec1-launch/\">Millions of dollars and 3.5 years, and it all came down to this</a></li>\n<li>Part 3: <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/30/tonal-ec1-community/\">Building online communities for fun, profit and product</a></li>\n<li>Part 4: <a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/30/tonal-ec1-future/\">Can Tonal become the luxury fitness market champion?</a></li>\n</ul>\n<p>We have more EC-1s in the works about other late-stage startups that are doing big things well and making news in the process.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"VP8MchqbLU\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/30/tonal-ec1/\">The Tonal EC-1</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;The Tonal EC-1&#8221; But the fact that a16z is pouring more capital into the alt-media space is not a surprise.</p>\n<p>Substack is a place where publications have bled some well-known talent, shifting the center of gravity in media. Let’s take a look at Substack’s historical growth.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"owHfdOjCkI\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/30/is-substack-really-worth-650m/\">Is Substack really worth $650M?</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Is Substack really worth $650M?&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/30/is-substack-really-worth-650m/embed/#?secret=owHfdOjCkI\" data-secret=\"owHfdOjCkI\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<h2>RPA market surges as investors, vendors capitalize on pandemic-driven tech shift</h2>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2132282\" style=\"width: 2131px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2132282\" loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-2132282 size-full\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg\" alt=\"Business process organization and analytics. Business process visualization and representation, automated workflow system concept. Vector concept creative illustration\" width=\"2121\" height=\"1414\" srcset=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg 2121w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg?resize=150,100 150w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg?resize=300,200 300w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg?resize=768,512 768w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg?resize=680,453 680w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg?resize=1536,1024 1536w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg?resize=2048,1365 2048w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1169397208-1.jpg?resize=50,33 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2121px) 100vw, 2121px\" /><p id=\"caption-attachment-2132282\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"><strong>Image Credits:</strong> Visual Generation / Getty Images</p></div></p>\n<p>Robotic process automation came to the fore during the pandemic as companies took steps to digitally transform. When employees couldn’t be in the same office together, it became crucial to cobble together more automated workflows that required fewer people in the loop.</p>\n<p>RPA has enabled executives to provide a level of automation that essentially buys them time to update systems to more modern approaches while reducing the large number of mundane manual tasks that are part of every industry’s workflow.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"GbybrO88HE\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/04/02/rpa-market-surges-investors-vendors-capitalize-pandemic-tech-shift/\">RPA market surges as investors, vendors capitalize on pandemic-driven tech shift</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;RPA market surges as investors, vendors capitalize on data-secret=\"GbybrO88HE\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<h2>E-commerce roll-ups are the next wave of disruption in consumer packaged goods</h2>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2129855\" style=\"width: 2130px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2129855\" loading=\"lazy\" 768w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1224334802.jpg?resize=680,454 680w, https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1224334802.jpg?resize=1536,1024 50w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2120px) 100vw, 2120px\" /><p id=\"caption-attachment-2129855\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"><strong>Image Credits:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.gettyimages.com/search/photographer?family=creative&#38;photographer=Javier+Zayas+Photography\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Javier Zayas Photography <span class=\"screen-reader-text\">(opens in a new window)</span></a> / Getty Images</p></div></p>\n<p>This year is all about the roll-ups, the aggregation of smaller companies into larger firms, creating a potentially compelling path for equity value. The interest in creating value through e-commerce brands is particularly striking.</p>\n<p>Just a year ago, digitally native brands had fallen out of favor with venture capitalists after so many failed to create venture-scale returns. As a result, edtech M&#38;A activity has continued to swell.</p>\n<p>The idea of a well-capitalized startup buying competitors to complement its core business is nothing new, but exits in this sector are notable because the money used to buy startups can be seen as an effect of the pandemic’s impact on remote education.</p>\n<p>But in the past week, the consolidation environment made a clear statement: Pandemic-proven startups are scooping up talent — and fast.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"2KiUhTtyHN\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/04/01/how-is-edtech-spending-its-extra-capital/\">How is edtech spending its extra capital?</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;How is edtech spending its extra capital?&#8221; Competition is afoot as well.</p>\n<p>Because of similar market conditions, Asian tech giants are directly expanding into Mexico and other LatAm countries.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"XmcwTw4dEo\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/04/01/tech-in-mexico-a-confluence-of-latin-america-the-us-and-asia/\">Tech in frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<h2>How we improved net retention by 30+ points in 2 quarters</h2>\n<p><div underrated metric out there.</p>\n<p>NRR is simply total revenue minus any revenue churn plus any revenue expansion from upgrades, cross-sells or upsells. The greater the NRR, the quicker companies can scale.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"oPRvrpsOal\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/26/how-our-saas-startup-improved-net-revenue-retention-by-more-than-30-points-in-two-quarters/\">How our SaaS startup improved net revenue retention by more than 30 points in two quarters</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;How our SaaS startup improved net revenue retention by more than 30 points in two quarters&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/26/how-our-saas-startup-improved-net-revenue-retention-by-more-than-30-points-in-two-quarters/embed/#?secret=oPRvrpsOal\" data-secret=\"oPRvrpsOal\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<h2>5 mistakes creators make building new games on Roblox</h2>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2130849\" style=\"width: 1034px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2130849\" loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-2130849 size-full\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1231917865.jpg\" alt=\"BRAZIL - 2021/03/24: In this photo illustration a Roblox logo seen displayed on a smartphone. When the pandemic hit, some people fled major metropolitan markets for smaller towns — raising questions about the future validity of cities.</p>\n<p>But those who predicted that COVID-19 would destroy major urban communities might want to stop shorting the resilience of these municipalities and start going long on what the post-pandemic future looks like.</p>\n<div class=\"embed breakout\">\n<blockquote class=\"wp-embedded-content\" data-secret=\"LpPZbW9QL5\"><p><a href=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/29/will-the-pandemic-spur-a-smart-rebirth-for-cities/\">Will the pandemic spur a smart rebirth for cities?</a></p></blockquote>\n<p><iframe class=\"wp-embedded-content\" sandbox=\"allow-scripts\" security=\"restricted\" title=\"&#8220;Will the pandemic spur a smart rebirth for cities?&#8221; &#8212; TechCrunch\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/2021/03/29/will-the-pandemic-spur-a-smart-rebirth-for-cities/embed/#?secret=LpPZbW9QL5\" data-secret=\"LpPZbW9QL5\" width=\"800\" height=\"450\" frameborder=\"0\" marginwidth=\"0\" marginheight=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\"></iframe></div>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<h2>The NFT craze will be a boon for lawyers</h2>\n<p><div id=\"attachment_2131276\" style=\"width: 2131px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-2131276\" loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-2131276 size-full\" src=\"https://techcrunch.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/GettyImages-1180199981.jpg\" alt=\"3d rendering of pink piggy bank standing on sounding block with gavel lying beside on light-blue background with copy space.
